The functionality of the amygdala has been explored through animal testing on rhesus monkeys, who had one side of symmetrical brain element removed and the brain’s hemispheres seperated.
The Difference in behavior was significant when either eye was covered:
With an open eye on the side of the intact amygdala, the monkeys’ reactions to potential threats or partners for (sexual) interactions were normal.
When the same eye was covered, however, the primates showed neither fear, nor aggression or empathy..
What if knowledge production no longer meant breaking open and illuminating bodies?
If enlightenment did not mean bringing light into the darkness. but if we would use other senses to imagine what we do when we produce knowledge.
what kind of knowledge would emerge, if we were to take the tentacles of the jellyfish for example as our model …
… where the visual, the haptic and the sexual meet?
Synchronicity, reaction time and perception time.
Rhetoric means like dicontinuous imagery, simple visualisations, cgi with tendencies, pop-ref as used by scholars of neuroscience.
A/V-Sync as a toll at the verge of rhythm or worldly coherence.
>Manifold arguments<
Motion extrapolation and latency difference, predictive, extrapolating the trajectory of a moving stimulus into the future.
or Neither but Postdictive
